[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika ThreeDXMLParser component. The fuzzer identified an attempted connection to an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during XML parsing operations, indicating that the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser processes external entity references without proper validation or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrestriction, potentially allowing attackers to trigger arbitrary network requests [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbased on untrusted input data.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium exception raised by the Jazzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity sanitizer during fuzzing operations. The vulnerability is classified as [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where the application attempts to establish [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork connections to destinations that may be controlled or influenced by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input data.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is a security vulnerability that allows an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker to cause the server-side application to make HTTP requests to arbitrary [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdomains. This can lead to:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltration of sensitive data from internal or external systems[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exposure of internal services and network architecture[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential for further attacks against internal infrastructure[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Data leakage through DNS queries or connection attempts[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The vulnerability originates in [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.parser.threedxml.ThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m141[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The parser processes a ZIP file through `[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParser.processZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParser.parseContent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The parsing delegates to the standard Java XML parser [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`javax.xml.parsers.SAXParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The SAX parser implementation processes the XML document through Xerces internal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. During entity reference scanning [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the parser encounters an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The entity manager attempts to resolve and fetch the external entity [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m677[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. This triggers an HTTPS connection attempt through Java's standard URL connection[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. The connection attempt to [0m[32m"jazzer.com:443"[0m[39m is intercepted by Jazzer's SSRF [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection sanitizer[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XML External Entity Processing**: The vulnerability occurs during XML entity [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference scanning, indicating that the parser processes external entities without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper restrictions. This is evident from the call to [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Network Connection Attempt**: The stack trace shows a complete HTTPS [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection setup sequence, from socket creation to SSL handshake preparation, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrating that the parser actually attempts to fetch external resources rather [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan just parsing entity declarations.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **3D XML Format Handling**: The vulnerability specifically affects the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser, which handles 3DXML format files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mappears to be ZIP-based archives[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining XML data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Default Parser Configuration**: The issue suggests that the SAXParser used in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser is likely configured with default settings that allow external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity resolution and processing.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m141[0m[39m where [0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is called[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m537[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m538[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m539[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability exists in the `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method of `ThreeDXMLParser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m123[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where a SAXParser is manually created without security configurations:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only namespace awareness is set[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Vulnerable to XXE/SSRF[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis implementation:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does NOT disable external entity resolution[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does NOT disable DTD loading[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does NOT set FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allows the parser to make arbitrary network requests when processing external [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace confirms that during XML parsing, the Xerces parser attempts to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve an external entity reference and establishes an HTTPS connection to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"jazzer.com:443"[0m[39m, triggering the SSRF detection.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inconsistency in Current Implementation[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Secure:** Line [0m[1;36m118[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for Manifest.xml parsing[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, manifestHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ✓ Secure[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerable:** Lines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m141[0m[39m use manual SAXParser creation for root XML parsing[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ✗ Vulnerable[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis inconsistency indicates the developer was aware of secure parsing utilities [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut failed to apply them uniformly.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Replace lines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m142[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:**[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specific changes:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Remove lines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m137[0m[39m:** Delete the manual SAXParserFactory and SAXParser [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation code[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Modify line [0m[1;36m139[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m142[0m[39m:** Replace `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Result:** The [0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method will use the same secure pattern as [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mprocessZip[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Security Guarantees:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` disables all external entity processing:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `external-general-entities = false` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents SSRF from general entities[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `external-parameter-entities = false`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `load-external-dtd = false`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `load-dtd-grammar = false`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING = true`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` adds Xerces SecurityManager with entity expansion[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimits[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` wraps the handler with `OfflineContentHandler` which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns empty streams for entity resolution[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserves Existing Functionality:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `RootHandler` extends `DefaultHandler` which implements `ContentHandler`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` accepts any `ContentHandler` implementation[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All SAX events [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstartElement, endElement, characters[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are delivered identically[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Metadata extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTitle, Author, Generator, Created[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continues to work[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Content extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39melement names from [0m[32m"name"[0m[39m attributes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continues to work[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing test `[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParserTest.testBasic[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will pass without [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Consistency with Tika Codebase:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- EpubParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39manother ZIP-based format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for all [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML parsing from ZIP entries[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- IWorkPackageParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39manother ZIP-based format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- DIFParser uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The same ThreeDXMLParser class already uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mManifest.xml at line [0m[1;36m118[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Minimal Code Changes:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m lines of vulnerable code[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Adds [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m line of secure code[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to method signatures or return types[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to exception handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaException is already in the throws clause[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No impact on other methods or classes[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Security Implications[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prevents the SSRF:**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen malicious XML contains external entity references like:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```xml[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<!DOCTYPE root [0m[1;39m[[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  <!ENTITY xxe SYSTEM [0m[32m"https://jazzer.com/malicious"[0m[39m>[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m][0m[39m>[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<root>&xxe;<[0m[35m/[0m[95mroot[0m[39m>[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerable code attempts to resolve the entity by:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` detects the entity [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` attempts to resolve it[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` opens an HTTPS connection to the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal URL[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Result:** SSRF vulnerability - arbitrary network request based on [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled input[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe secure code prevents this by:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SAXParserFactory level:** Feature `external-general-entities = false` tells [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parser to NOT resolve external entities[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **OfflineContentHandler level:** If an entity resolution is somehow attempted, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mresolveEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns an empty InputStream[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Result:** No network connection is made, SSRF is prevented[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected** for legitimate 3DXML files, as they should not contain external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If a 3DXML file legitimately uses external entities [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhighly unlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, those [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities will be silently ignored[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If a 3DXML file has malicious external entities, they will be blocked [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdesired [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Impact:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing test `[0m[1;35mThreeDXMLParserTest.testBasic[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` tests a legitimate 3DXML file[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand will continue to pass[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to test code are required[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Additional tests for XXE/SSRF protection can be added [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimilar to [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TestXXEInXML.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Performance Impact:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses a parser pool for efficiency[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Performance may actually improve slightly due to parser reuse[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No negative performance impact expected[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m:** Open [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-cad-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.java`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:** Locate the `[0m[1;35mparseRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m123[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Why This Fix Does Not Violate Constraints[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Does NOT modify fuzzing logic:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is not modified[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix is in the source code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ThreeDXMLParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not the test harness[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The same API [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is called by the fuzzer[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Does NOT modify external libraries:**[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `XMLReaderUtils` is part of tika-core, not an external library[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No modifications to Xerces, SAXParser, or other XML libraries[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Does NOT break existing tests:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing test uses legitimate 3DXML files without external entities[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `RootHandler` interface remains unchanged[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All metadata extraction and content parsing logic is preserved[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Does NOT remove functionality:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XML parsing still occurs[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All SAX events are delivered to RootHandler[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Metadata extraction continues to work[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is a security hardening, not a feature removal[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m. Comparison with Similar Fixes in Tika[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe proposed fix follows the exact pattern used to secure other XML parsers in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **TIKA-[0m[1;36m185[0m[39m:** Introduced `OfflineContentHandler` to prevent XXE attacks[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **EpubParser:** Uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for all XML parsing from ZIP [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **IWorkPackageParser:** Uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for all XML parsing[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **DIFParser:** Uses `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for all XML parsing[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis demonstrates that the fix is a well-established pattern in the Tika codebase.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
